I caught it. I heard about this drug. I said, \xe2\x80\x98Let me take it.\xe2\x80\x99 It was my suggestion. I said, \xe2\x80\x98Let me take it,\xe2\x80\x99 and it was incredible the way it worked, incredible.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>While hospitalized at Walter Reed Medical Center, Trump began a course of an experimental antibody cocktail manufactured by Regeneron last Saturday. The president had been admitted to the hospital after experiencing multiple drops in his blood oxygen level on Friday, the day after he said he first tested positive for COVID-19. Not approved by the FDA for use for COVID-19 patients, the drug costs over $100,000 per year for patients who take it to fight cancer and blood disorders.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cI spent four days there,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said of Walter Reed, \xe2\x80\x9cand I went in, I wasn\xe2\x80\x99t feeling so hot, and within a very short period of time they gave me Regeneron, it\xe2\x80\x99s called Regeneron, and other things too, but I think this was the key but they gave me Regeneron and it was like unbelievable.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>Without specifying how he would go about it, Trump said he hoped to get the medication, as well as another made by pharmaceutical manufacturer Eli Lilly, approved by the FDA and provided free of charge to all hospitalized COVID-19 patients in America.</p><div class="caas-readmore caas-readmore-collapse"><button class="link rapid-noclick-resp caas-button collapse-button" aria-label="" title="" data-ylk="elm:readmore;slk:Story continues">Story continues</button></div><p>\xe2\x80\x9cWe\xe2\x80\x99re trying to get them on an emergency basis,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said. \xe2\x80\x9cWe\xe2\x80\x99ve authorized it. I\xe2\x80\x99ve authorized it and if you\xe2\x80\x99re in the hospital and you\xe2\x80\x99re feeling really bad, I think we\xe2\x80\x99re going to work it so that you\xe2\x80\x99re going to get them and you\xe2\x80\x99re going to get them free.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>Echoing statements he has <a href="https://news.yahoo.com/president-trump-announces-leaving-walter-reed-hospital-covid-185628667.html" data-ylk="slk:made since returning;outcm:mb_qualified_link;_E:mb_qualified_link;ct:story;" class="link rapid-noclick-resp yahoo-link">made since returning</a> to the White House from Walter Reed, Trump assured the nation that the more than 7 million Americans infected with the virus could easily beat it.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cYou\xe2\x80\x99re going to get better. You\xe2\x80\x99re going to get better really fast,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said.</p><p>Trump likely <a href="https://news.yahoo.com/trump-likely-remains-infectious-for-covid-19-and-may-still-be-for-the-next-debate-with-biden-195554634.html" data-ylk="slk:remains infectious;outcm:mb_qualified_link;_E:mb_qualified_link;ct:story;" class="link rapid-noclick-resp yahoo-link">remains infectious</a> for COVID-19. The CDC states on its website that patients with mild to moderate cases of the disease remain contagious for at least 10 days, while those with more severe cases can still transmit it for up to 20 days.</p><figure class="caas-figure"><div class="caas-figure-with-pb" style="max-height: 396.5625px"><div class="caas-img-container caas-img-loader" style="padding-bottom:56%;"><img class="caas-img caas-lazy has-preview" alt="President Trump delivers a videotaped message outside the Oval Office. (Photo courtesy the White House) " src="https://s.yimg.com/ny/api/res/1.2/Hr8f_SpFCbNmmtrQ5E6owA--/YXBwaWQ9aGlnaGxhbmRlcjt3PTcwNTtoPTM5Ni41NjI1/https://s.yimg.com/uu/api/res/1.2/8cywe27ZWAwXkw.z0KMVJQ--~B/aD03NTY7dz0xMzQ0O3NtPTE7YXBwaWQ9eXRhY2h5b24-/https://media-mbst-pub-ue1.s3.amazonaws.com/creatr-uploaded-images/2020-10/6f712a40-08f1-11eb-bddf-95ee8675c563" class="caas-img"></noscript></div></div><figcaption class="caption-collapse">President Trump delivers a videotaped message outside the Oval Office. (Photo courtesy the White House)</figcaption></figure><p>Trump admitted that his goal of having a vaccine for COVID-19 in distribution by the Nov. 3 election was not achievable. He blamed \xe2\x80\x9cpolitics\xe2\x80\x9d for getting in the way.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cWe\xe2\x80\x99re going to have a great vaccine very, very shortly,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said. \xe2\x80\x9cI think we should have it before the election but frankly the politics gets involved and that\xe2\x80\x99s OK. They want to play their games. It\xe2\x80\x99s going to be right after the election.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>The Food and Drug Administration informed drug manufacturers this week that they would need at least two months of follow-up data to show that their vaccines were safe for the general public. That timeline means that a vaccine will not be ready before Election Day.</p><p>Trump then took credit for the pace at which the vaccine has been developed, saying that his pressure on the FDA had made the difference.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cNo president has ever pushed them like I pushed them,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said.</p><p>Former Vice President <a href="https://news.yahoo.com/biden-if-trump-still-has-covid-19-we-shouldnt-have-a-debate-235938033.html" data-ylk="slk:Joe Biden;outcm:mb_qualified_link;_E:mb_qualified_link;ct:story;" class="link rapid-noclick-resp yahoo-link">Joe Biden</a> was asked by reporters in Wilmington, Del., to respond to Trump\xe2\x80\x99s assertion that catching COVID-19&nbsp; was a \xe2\x80\x9cblessing in disguise.\xe2\x80\x9d&nbsp; \xe2\x80\x9cI\xe2\x80\x99m going to think before I speak. I think it\xe2\x80\x99s a tragedy the president deals with COVID like it is something not to be worried about when already 210,000 people have died,\xe2\x80\x9d Biden responded.</p><p><strong>_____</strong></p><p>&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Read more from Yahoo News:</strong></p><ul class="caas-list caas-list-bullet"><li><p><a Not approved by the FDA for use for COVID-19 patients, the drug costs over $100,000 per year for patients who take it to fight cancer and blood disorders.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\u003Cp\\u003E\xe2\x80\x9cI spent four days there,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said of Walter Reed, \xe2\x80\x9cand I went in, I wasn\xe2\x80\x99t feeling so hot, and within a very short period of time they gave me Regeneron, it\xe2\x80\x99s called Regeneron, and other things too, but I think this was the key but they gave me Regeneron and it was like unbelievable.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\u003Cp\\u003EWithout specifying how he would go about it, Trump said he hoped to get the medication, as well as another made by pharmaceutical manufacturer Eli Lilly, approved by the FDA and provided free of charge to all hospitalized COVID-19 patients in America.\\u003C\\u002Fp\\u003E\\u003Cdiv class=\\"caas-readmore caas-readmore-collapse\\"\\u003E\\u003Cbutton class=\\"link rapid-noclick-resp caas-button collapse-button\\" aria-label=\\"\\" title=\\"\\" data-ylk=\\"elm:readmore;slk:Story continues\\"\\u003EStory continues\\u003C\\u002Fbutton\\u003E\\u003C\\u002Fdiv\\u003E\\u003Cp\\u003E\xe2\x80\x9cWe\xe2\x80\x99re trying to get them on an emergency basis,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said. \xe2\x80\x9cWe\xe2\x80\x99ve authorized it.
